58    "\n",
59    "\n",
60    "## Definition of the N-body problem\n",
61    "\n",
62    "In Nbody.jl below, the following functions are defined: NbodyEnergy(u,Gm), NbodyODE!(du,u,Gm,t), and NbodyODE1!(du,u,Gm,t), where\n",
63    "\n",
64    "\\begin{equation*}\n",
65    "u = \n",
66    "\\left(\\begin{matrix}\n",
67    "q_1  & v_1\\\\\n",
68    "\\vdots & \\vdots \\\\\n",
69    "q_N  & v_N\n",
70    "\\end{matrix}\n",
71    "\\right) \\in \\mathbb{R}^{2 \\times 3\\times N}, \\quad\n",
72    "Gm = (G\\,  m_1, \\ldots,G\\,  m_N) \\in \\mathbb{R}^N.\n",
73    "\\end{equation*}"
74   ]
75  },
76  {
77   "cell_type": "markdown",
78   "metadata": {},
79   "source": [
80    "The energy, as a function of the positions $q_1,\\ldots,q_N \\in \\mathbb{R}^3$ and the velocities $v_1,\\ldots,v_N \\in \\mathbb{R}^3$ of the $N$ bodies is:\n",
81    "\\begin{equation*}\n",
82    "\\begin{split}\n",
83    "\\mathrm{Energy}(q_1,\\ldots,q_N,v_1,\\ldots,v_N) = \n",
84    "\\frac12 \\sum_{i=1}^{N} m_i \\, \\|v_i\\|^2\n",
85    "- G \\sum_{1\\leq i < j \\leq N} \\frac{m_i m_j}{\\|q_i-q_j\\|}.\n",
86    "\\end{split}\n",
87    "\\end{equation*}\n",
88    "\n",
89    "\n",
90    "The ODE system of the N-body problem,\n",
91    "as a function of the positions $q_1,\\ldots,q_N \\in \\mathbb{R}^3$ and the velocities $v_1,\\ldots,v_N \\in \\mathbb{R}^3$ of the $N$ bodies is:\n",
92    "\\begin{equation*}\n",
93    "\\begin{split}\n",
94    "\\frac{d}{dt} q_i &= v_i, \\\\\n",
95    "\\frac{d}{dt} v_i &= G\\, \n",
96    "\\sum_{j \\neq i} \\frac{m_j}{\\|q_j-q_i\\|^3}\\,\n",
97    "(q_j-q_i).\n",
98    "\\end{split}\n",
99    "\\end{equation*}\n",
100    "This system of ODEs can be writen in compact form as\n",
101    "\\begin{equation*}\n",
102    "\\frac{d u}{dt} = f(t,u,Gm)\n",
103    "\\end{equation*}\n",
104    "\n",
105    "\n"
106   ]
107  },
108  {
109   "cell_type": "code",
110   "execution_count": 4,
111   "metadata": {},
112   "outputs": [

1002    "yrange = (1e-16,1e-4)\n",
1003    "year = 365.5\n",
1004    "\n",
1005    "function energy_plot(sol; title=\"\")\n",
1006    "    energies = [NbodyEnergy(BigFloat.(u),Gm) for u in sol.u]\n",
1007    "    E0 = energies[1]\n",
1008    "    epsilon = eps(1e-3)\n",
1009    "    errors = Float64.(abs.(energies[2:end]/E0 .- 1)) .+ epsilon\n",
1010    "    tt = sol.t[2:end]  #/year\n",
1011    "    pl = plot(title=title,\n",
1012    "         yscale=:log10, legend=false) #ylims=yrange, \n",
1013    "    plot!(tt,  errors)\n",
1014    "    return pl\n",
1015    "end\n",
1016    "\n",
1017    "\n",
1018    "pl1 = energy_plot(sol1, title=\"IRKGL_simd_berria\")\n",
1019    "\n",
1020    "pl2 = energy_plot(sol2, title=\"IRKGL_simd\")\n",
1021    "\n",
